{"Quotes": "[1] \"Light olefins including ethylene and propylene are important building block molecules for the synthesis of downstream chemical products and intermediates\"\n\n[2] \"Propylene is traditionally produced as a by-product by the cracking of naphtha and coal, which cannot meet the expanded market demand anymore.\"\n\n[3] \"On the other hand, the exploit of unconventional natural gas like shale gas provides abundant and cheap light alkane sources\"\n\n[4] \"The main production propylene through propane dehydrogenation (PDH) reaction becomes very effective and competitive due to the following advantages such as single feed (propane), single product (propylene), wide source of raw materials, and low cost\"\n\n[5] \"The challenges are still from the improvements of coke resistance and anti-sintering of active sites under the reaction conditions since propane dehydrogenation is an endothermic reaction.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology has emerged as the most promising method for propylene production due to several key advantages:\n\n1. Single feedstock and product: PDH uses only propane as input and produces propylene as the main product, simplifying the process.\n\n2. Abundant and cheap raw materials: The exploitation of unconventional natural gas sources like shale gas has made propane widely available at low costs.\n\n3. Wide availability of feedstock: Propane is available from various sources.\n\n4. Cost-effectiveness: The simple process and cheap feedstock make PDH a low-cost production route.\n\n5. Meeting growing demand: Unlike traditional by-product methods from naphtha and coal cracking, PDH can meet the expanding market demand for propylene.\n\n6. Process efficiency: As a direct conversion process, PDH offers higher efficiency than conventional multi-step methods.\n\n7. Improved selectivity: The single-product nature of PDH allows for better control and higher selectivity towards propylene.\n\nThese advantages make PDH technology particularly suited to address the challenges of feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional propylene production methods. However, PDH still faces challenges in improving coke resistance and preventing sintering of active sites due to the endothermic nature of the reaction.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术因其多项关键优势而成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 单一原料和产品：PDH仅使用丙烷作为输入，主要产品为丙烯，简化了生产过程。\n\n2. 原料丰富且价格低廉：非常规天然气（如页岩气）的开发提供了丰富且价格低廉的轻烃资源，包括丙烷。\n\n3. 原料来源广泛：丙烷可从多种来源获得。\n\n4. 成本效益：简单的工艺和廉价的原料使PDH成为一种低成本的生产路线。\n\n5. 满足不断增长的需求：与传统的石脑油和煤炭裂解副产品方法不同，PDH可以满足不断扩大的丙烯市场需求。\n\n6. 工艺效率高：作为一种直接转化工艺，PDH比传统多步骤方法提供了更高的效率。\n\n7. 产品选择性高：PDH的单一产品特性使其能够实现更好的控制和对丙烯的高选择性。\n\n这些优势使PDH技术特别适合解决传统丙烯生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战。然而，由于反应的吸热性质，PDH仍面临着提高抗积碳性和防止活性位点烧结的挑战。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.mcat.2021.112081"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Propylene serves as one of the most significant compounds in the chemical industry. Propane dehydrogenation (PDH), an on purpose propylene production technology is developing.\"\n\n[2] \"As an endothermic process, high operation temperatures and harsh conditions extensively limit the catalyst development.\"\n\n[3] \"Pt- and CrOx-based catalysts have been applied in commercialized PDH processes on account of their excellent activity and propylene productivity.\"\n\n[4] \"Among propylene production processes, propane dehydrogenation (PDH), (57) a process of direct conversion of propane into propylene and hydrogen is considered to be one of the most promising propylene production methods compared with methanol-to-olefins, FischerTropsch-to-olefins, etc.\"\n\n[5] \"PDH requires operation at high temperatures (generally above 500 C), which restricts the C3H6 selectivity and catalyst structure stability on account of coking side reactions, particle sintering, and so forth.\"\n\n[6] \"Chemical looping oxidative dehydrogenation (CL-ODH) as an alternative propylene production technologies can break through the thermodynamic equilibrium limitation of nonoxidative dehydrogenation.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. On-purpose production: PDH is specifically designed to produce propylene, allowing for targeted and efficient production to meet growing demand.\n\n2. Feedstock availability and flexibility: PDH uses propane as a feedstock, which is more readily available and potentially less expensive compared to traditional feedstocks like naphtha or ethane.\n\n3. Process efficiency: PDH involves the direct conversion of propane to propylene, potentially offering higher yields and efficiency compared to more complex multi-step processes like methanol-to-olefins or Fischer-Tropsch-to-olefins.\n\n4. Product selectivity: PDH technology allows for high selectivity towards propylene production, as it is designed specifically for this purpose.\n\n5. Independence from petroleum refining: Unlike steam cracking, PDH is not tied to petroleum refining, allowing for more flexible production.\n\n6. Potential for further improvements: Ongoing research in catalyst development (e.g., Pt- and CrOx-based catalysts) and process optimization promises to further enhance PDH efficiency and selectivity.\n\nHowever, PDH technology also faces challenges:\n\n1. High energy requirements: As an endothermic process, it requires high temperatures (generally above 500°C), which can limit catalyst development and increase operational costs.\n\n2. Catalyst deactivation: Issues like coking, sintering, and other side reactions can affect catalyst longevity and performance.\n\n3. Thermodynamic limitations: The equilibrium conversion is limited at high temperatures, requiring innovative reactor designs or process modifications to overcome this constraint.\n\n4. Cost considerations: Some effective catalysts, like Pt-based ones, are expensive, driving research into more cost-effective alternatives.\n\nDespite these challenges, PDH remains a promising technology due to its ability to produce high-purity propylene efficiently, addressing the limitations of conventional production methods in terms of feedstock flexibility and product selectivity. Additionally, alternative technologies like chemical looping oxidative dehydrogenation (CL-ODH) are being developed to overcome some of the limitations of traditional PDH processes.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH专门设计用于生产丙烯，允许有针对性和高效率的生产以满足不断增长的需求。\n\n2. 原料可用性和灵活性：PDH使用丙烷作为原料，与传统的原料如石脑油或乙烷相比，丙烷更容易获得且可能更便宜。\n\n3. 工艺效率：PDH涉及丙烷到丙烯的直接转化，与更复杂的多步骤过程（如甲醇制烯烃或费托制烯烃）相比，可能提供更高的产率和效率。\n\n4. 产品选择性：PDH技术允许高选择性地生产丙烯，因为它专门为此目的而设计。\n\n5. 独立于石油精炼：与蒸汽裂解不同，PDH不依赖于石油精炼，允许更灵活的生产。\n\n6. 进一步改进的潜力：正在进行的催化剂开发（如基于Pt和CrOx的催化剂）和工艺优化研究有望进一步提高PDH的效率和选择性。\n\n然而，PDH技术也面临一些挑战：\n\n1. 高能耗要求：作为一个吸热过程，它需要高温（通常高于500°C），这可能会限制催化剂的开发并增加运营成本。\n\n2. 催化剂失活：结焦、烧结和其他副反应等问题可能影响催化剂的寿命和性能。\n\n3. 热力学限制：在高温下平衡转化率受到限制，需要创新的反应器设计或工艺改进来克服这一约束。\n\n4. 成本考虑：一些有效的催化剂，如基于铂的催化剂，价格昂贵，推动了对更具成本效益的替代品的研究。\n\n尽管存在这些挑战，PDH仍然是一项有前景的技术，因为它能够高效地生产高纯度丙烯，解决了传统生产方法在原料灵活性和产品选择性方面的限制。此外，正在开发化学链氧化脱氢（CL-ODH）等替代技术，以克服传统PDH工艺的一些局限性。", "Doi": "10.1021/accountsmr.0c00012"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Recently, propane dehydrogenation has been widely investigated as an effective approach to propene production because of the continuing decrease in fossil oil resources and the increasing market for propene\"\n\n[2] \"Low-cost saturated hydrocarbons can be converted to value-added olefins by propane dehydrogenation, and this route is economically competitive\"\n\n[3] \"Propane dehydrogenation is a highly endothermic and equilibrium-limited reaction, therefore a high temperature is needed to obtain a satisfactory yield of propene\"\n\n[4] \"However, problems such as hydrocarbon cracking and coke formation arise with increasing reaction temperature, and these lead to decreases in the activity and stability of the catalyst\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. Feedstock availability: PDH directly uses propane, which is abundantly available from natural gas processing and oil refining. This addresses the challenge of decreasing fossil oil resources faced by conventional production methods.\n\n2. Economic competitiveness: PDH converts low-cost saturated hydrocarbons (propane) into higher-value olefins (propylene), making it an economically attractive route.\n\n3. Process efficiency: PDH is a more direct and efficient route to produce propylene compared to traditional methods like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n4. Product selectivity: PDH can achieve high propylene selectivity, potentially over 90%, which is significantly higher than conventional methods. This addresses the challenge of improving product yield and reducing byproduct formation.\n\n5. Flexibility: PDH plants can be scaled and located close to propane sources or propylene consumers, offering flexibility in production and distribution.\n\nHowever, PDH technology also faces some challenges:\n\n1. High energy requirement: The process is highly endothermic, requiring high temperatures to achieve satisfactory propylene yields.\n\n2. Catalyst deactivation: The high temperatures can lead to hydrocarbon cracking and coke formation, which decrease catalyst activity and stability.\n\n3. Equilibrium limitations: The reaction is equilibrium-limited, which can affect overall conversion rates.\n\nDespite these challenges, ongoing research into improved catalysts and process designs is making PDH an increasingly attractive option for addressing the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 原料可用性：PDH直接使用丙烷，这种原料可以从天然气加工和石油精炼中大量获得。这解决了传统生产方法面临的化石油资源减少的挑战。\n\n2. 经济竞争力：PDH将低成本的饱和烃（丙烷）转化为高价值的烯烃（丙烯），使其成为一种经济上有吸引力的路线。\n\n3. 工艺效率：与蒸汽裂解或流化催化裂解等传统方法相比，PDH是一种更直接、更高效的丙烯生产路线。\n\n4. 产品选择性：PDH可以实现高丙烯选择性，潜在地超过90%，这显著高于传统方法。这解决了提高产品产率和减少副产品形成的挑战。\n\n5. 灵活性：PDH装置可以根据需要进行规模调整，并且可以靠近丙烷来源或丙烯消费者，提供生产和分配上的灵活性。\n\n然而，PDH技术也面临一些挑战：\n\n1. 高能耗要求：该过程是高度吸热的，需要高温才能获得令人满意的丙烯产率。\n\n2. 催化剂失活：高温可能导致烃类裂解和焦炭形成，这会降低催化剂的活性和稳定性。\n\n3. 平衡限制：反应受平衡限制，可能影响整体转化率。\n\n尽管存在这些挑战，但对改进催化剂和工艺设计的持续研究正使PDH成为一个越来越有吸引力的选择，以满足不断增长的全球丙烯需求。", "Doi": "10.1016/S1872-2067(17)62805-5"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Propylene is one of the most important petrochemical building blocks for the production of a diverse range of products, from solvents to plastics and other valuable intermediates, for example, polypropylene, acrylonitrile, acrolein, and acrylic acid.\"\n\n[2] \"Because of an increasing demand of propylene and the depletion of petroleum resources, on-purposed propylene production technologies from alternative substrates, such as methanol-to-olefin (MTO), [3,4] metathesis of ethylene and butylene [5] and propane dehydrogenation (PDH) [6] have been intensively developed.\"\n\n[3] \"Among these technologies, propane dehydrogenation is the most economical and shortest route for propylene production and is commercially available, developed by several licensing processes including the Catofin process from CB&I Lummus, reference [7] and the Oleflex process from Universal Oil Products (or Honeywell UOP) [8].\"\n\n[4] \"Because this reaction is a highly endothermic process and equilibrium-limited reaction, the relatively high temperature (above 550 C) is usually required for promoting the catalytic activity. Thus, this behavior facilitates several side-reactions, in particular, thermal/catalytic cracking and coke formation, resulting in the low propylene selectivity and the rapid deactivation of catalysts [9].\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. Economic efficiency: PDH is described as the most economical route for propylene production among alternative technologies.\n\n2. Process simplicity: It is referred to as the \"shortest route\" for propylene production, suggesting a more straightforward process compared to other methods.\n\n3. Commercial viability: PDH technology is already commercially available and has been developed into licensed processes by major companies.\n\n4. Feedstock flexibility: As an on-purpose technology, PDH addresses the challenge of petroleum resource depletion by utilizing propane as a feedstock, which can be sourced from natural gas or other alternatives.\n\n5. Targeted production: Unlike conventional methods where propylene is obtained as a byproduct, PDH is specifically designed for propylene production, potentially offering better control over output.\n\nHowever, PDH technology also faces challenges:\n\n1. High energy requirements: The process is highly endothermic and requires high temperatures (above 550°C).\n\n2. Equilibrium limitations: The reaction is equilibrium-limited, which can affect overall efficiency.\n\n3. Side reactions: The high temperatures facilitate unwanted side reactions, particularly thermal/catalytic cracking and coke formation.\n\n4. Selectivity issues: These side reactions can result in low propylene selectivity.\n\n5. Catalyst deactivation: Rapid deactivation of catalysts is a significant challenge in PDH processes.\n\nDespite these challenges, PDH technology's advantages in terms of economic efficiency, process simplicity, and feedstock flexibility make it a promising solution to address the growing global demand for propylene, especially in the face of depleting petroleum resources and the limitations of conventional production methods.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 经济效率：PDH被描述为替代技术中最经济的丙烯生产路线。\n\n2. 工艺简单：它被称为丙烯生产的\"最短路线\"，表明与其他方法相比，工艺更加直接。\n\n3. 商业可行性：PDH技术已经商业化，并已被主要公司开发成为许可工艺。\n\n4. 原料灵活性：作为一种定向技术，PDH通过利用丙烷作为原料来解决石油资源枯竭的挑战，而丙烷可以从天然气或其他替代品中获得。\n\n5. 目标生产：与传统方法中丙烯作为副产品获得不同，PDH是专门为丙烯生产而设计的，可能提供更好的产出控制。\n\n然而，PDH技术也面临一些挑战：\n\n1. 高能耗要求：该过程是高度吸热的，需要高温（550°C以上）。\n\n2. 平衡限制：反应受平衡限制，可能影响整体效率。\n\n3. 副反应：高温会促进不需要的副反应，特别是热/催化裂解和焦炭形成。\n\n4. 选择性问题：这些副反应可能导致丙烯选择性低。\n\n5. 催化剂失活：催化剂的快速失活是PDH过程中的一个重大挑战。\n\n尽管存在这些挑战，PDH技术在经济效率、工艺简单性和原料灵活性方面的优势使其成为解决全球日益增长的丙烯需求的有前景的解决方案，特别是在面对石油资源枯竭和传统生产方法局限性的情况下。", "Doi": "10.3390/catal9020174"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Dehydrogenation of propane (DHP) is one of the on-purpose propylene production technologies that has received much attention in the recent past due to it's potential to make-up the shortfall of propylene supply left by conventional crackers (e.g., FCC)\"\n\n[2] \"Propylene is an important building block in a myriad of (petro)chemical applications, for instance in the production of polypropylene\"\n\n[3] \"However, major challenges associated with this catalytic system are cracking and coking which influence the product selectivity and catalyst stability, respectively. Thus, the deactivated catalyst must frequently be regenerated without losing dehydrogenation activity, selectivity to propylene and catalyst stability, which makes the process not only complex but also expensive.\"\n\n[4] \"Typically, the CrOxAl2O3 catalyst system is used for industrial processes, for example in the Catofin process (ABB Lummus) that runs at cyclic operation (reaction and regeneration) at 850 K\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it a promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. On-purpose production: PDH allows for targeted propylene production to address supply shortfalls from conventional crackers like fluid catalytic cracking (FCC).\n\n2. Feedstock flexibility: It utilizes propane as feedstock, which is more readily available compared to the naphtha or ethane used in steam cracking.\n\n3. Process efficiency: As a direct conversion process, PDH can potentially offer higher efficiency compared to cracking methods that produce multiple products.\n\n4. Product selectivity: PDH is more selective towards propylene production compared to cracking processes.\n\n5. Scalability: PDH units can be built at various scales to meet specific market demands.\n\n6. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Among the emerging methods, the PDH process has garnered interest as the most efficient process that can meet the large demand for propylene\"\n\n[2] \"A major problem of the PDH process, however, is that the reaction requires high-temperature operations, at 773 K or higher, to increase the thermodynamic equilibrium limit\"\n\n[3] \"Until recent years, the industrial demand for ethylene and propylene was satisfied with a balance by large-scale production from naphtha crackers\"\n\n[4] \"However, a new and less expensive source of ethylene recently became available in increasing amounts from ethane cracking in natural gas and shale gas\"\n\n[5] \"This broke the previous ethylene-propylene production balance, causing a need to find proper on-purpose methods for propylene production, such as catalytic propane dehydrogenation (PDH), olefin metathesis, and methanol-to-olefin processes\"\n\n[6] \"Typically, the PDH process employs a Pt-Sn bimetallic catalyst supported on porous alumina (PtSn/Al2O3) or chromium oxide-supported alumina (CrOx/Al2O3), but both suffer from rapid deactivation due to coke deposition\"\n\n[7] \"Of the two typical catalysts, CrOx/Al2O3 has disadvantages of chromium toxicity and rapid deactivation (approximately in 15 min), which can be overcome by catalyst regeneration by a simple air-burning process\"\n\n[8] \"On the other hand, the employed PtSn/Al2O3 catalyst requires frequent regeneration (typically, every 5 d), but the regeneration involves a high-temperature treatment with a toxic and corrosive gas mixture containing O2 and HCl\"", "English": "The key advantages of propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology that make it the most promising method for propylene production are:\n\n1. {"Quotes": "\"Direct dehydrogenation can be performed either with or without an oxidant present, and O2, CO2 and N2O can all participate as oxidants to form propene from propane. The discovery of active and selective catalysts is central to the development of these on-purpose technologies and is the focus of the current review.\"\n\n\"Annual propene production was around 130 megatonnes in 2019 and is predicted to increase to 191 megatonnes by 2030. Significantly, the expected growth in propane demand cannot be met by existing processes, which are based on steam-cracking (SC) and fluid catalytic cracking (FCC). Instead, direct or on-purpose processes are being developed to fill the so-called propene gap.\"\n\n\"The direct formation of propene from propane is a well-established commercial process, which on the basis of energy consumption, is environmentally preferred to the current large-scale sources of propene from steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking.\"\n\n\"At present, sources of propane are mostly non-renewable, but the development of technologies to produce renewable green propane are gaining traction, which coupled with new catalytic processes will provide the platform to produce green propene.\"\n\n\"Direct propane dehydrogenation satisfies many principles of green chemistry in comparison to SC and MTO benchmarks: it is highly atom-economic, does not use toxic reactants (or generate toxic by-products) and can in principle, utilise renewable feedstocks.\"\n\n\"DDH is to date the only reaction that has been operated commercially. The most active catalysts reported in the literature are based on chromium oxide or platinum promoted with tin oxide, but even these require frequent regeneration due to coking.\"\n\n\"In the case of dehydrogenation only H2 is generated as a by-product, meaning an atom economy of 95% is possible.\"\n\n\"From an environmental perspective, ODH-CO2 has the greatest potential in the context of a circular economy. Although the formation of water is less desirable than hydrogen, ODH-CO2 has the benefit of consuming CO2 in the process, and this is often cited as the motivation for investigating this route.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. On-purpose production: PDH is specifically designed to produce propylene, addressing the growing demand that cannot be met by existing processes like steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n2. Energy efficiency: PDH is more environmentally friendly in terms of energy consumption compared to traditional methods.\n\n3. Feedstock flexibility: PDH can utilize propane from various sources, including potential renewable sources in the future.\n\n4. High atom economy: PDH has a very high atom economy of up to 95%, making it highly efficient in terms of raw material utilization.\n\n5. Environmental benefits: PDH does not use toxic reactants or generate toxic by-products, and it can potentially use renewable feedstocks.\n\n6. Process flexibility: PDH can be performed with or without oxidants, allowing for process optimization based on specific requirements.\n\n7. Commercial viability: PDH is the only direct dehydrogenation process that has been successfully commercialized.\n\n8. Catalyst innovation: Ongoing research into active and selective catalysts is improving the efficiency and selectivity of PDH processes.\n\n9. Potential for sustainability: PDH technology can be coupled with emerging green propane production methods to create a more sustainable propylene production process.\n\nThese advantages address the challenges faced by conventional production methods in terms of feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity. PDH offers a more targeted, efficient, and potentially sustainable approach to propylene production, with the flexibility to adapt to changing feedstock availability and environmental concerns.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH专门设计用于生产丙烯，解决了现有工艺如蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解无法满足的不断增长的需求。\n\n2. 能源效率：与传统方法相比，PDH在能源消耗方面更加环保。\n\n3. 原料灵活性：PDH可以利用来自各种来源的丙烷，包括未来潜在的可再生来源。\n\n4. 高原子经济性：PDH具有高达95%的原子经济性，使其在原材料利用方面非常高效。\n\n5. 环境效益：PDH不使用有毒反应物或产生有毒副产品，并且可以潜在地使用可再生原料。\n\n6. 工艺灵活性：PDH可以在有或没有氧化剂的情况下进行，允许根据具体要求进行工艺优化。\n\n7. 商业可行性：PDH是唯一成功商业化的直接脱氢工艺。\n\n8. 催化剂创新：对活性和选择性催化剂的持续研究正在提高PDH工艺的效率和选择性。\n\n9. 可持续性潜力：PDH技术可以与新兴的绿色丙烷生产方法相结合，创造更可持续的丙烯生产工艺。\n\n这些优势解决了传统生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战。PDH提供了一种更有针对性、更高效和潜在更可持续的丙烯生产方法，具有适应不断变化的原料供应和环境问题的灵活性。", "Doi": "10.1039/D1GC03700E"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Noble-metal alloys are widely used as heterogeneous catalysts. However, due to the existence of scaling properties of adsorption energies on transition metal surfaces, the enhancement of catalytic activity is frequently accompanied by side reactions leading to a reduction in selectivity for the target product.\"\n\n          [2] \"Herein, we describe an approach to breaking the scaling relationship for propane dehydrogenation, an industrially important reaction, by assembling single atom alloys (SAAs), to achieve simultaneous enhancement of propylene selectivity and propane conversion.\"\n\n          [3] \"Unlike previous reported SAA applications at low temperatures (<400C), Pt/Cu SAA shows excellent stability of more than 120h of operation under atmospheric pressure at 520C.\"", "English": "The key advantages of propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology for propylene production include:\n\n          1. Breaking the scaling relationship: PDH using single atom alloys (SAAs) can simultaneously enhance propylene selectivity and propane conversion, overcoming the trade-off between activity and selectivity faced by conventional catalysts.\n\n          2. High selectivity and conversion: SAA catalysts, particularly Pt/Cu SAA, can achieve high propylene selectivity while maintaining good conversion rates.\n\n          3. Excellent stability at high temperatures: Pt/Cu SAA catalysts demonstrate exceptional stability, operating for over 120 hours at high temperatures (520°C) under atmospheric pressure. This is a significant improvement over previous SAA applications that were limited to lower temperatures.\n\n          4. Improved efficiency: By breaking the scaling relationship, PDH technology addresses the challenge of side reactions that typically reduce selectivity in conventional methods.\n\n          5. Process simplification: Direct dehydrogenation of propane to propylene is a simpler process compared to conventional methods like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n          6. Cost-effectiveness: The use of single atom alloys with a low platinum loading (0.1wt%) on copper nanoparticles suggests a potentially more cost-effective catalyst compared to traditional platinum-based catalysts.\n\n          These advantages directly address the challenges of feedstock utilization efficiency, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional propylene production methods, making PDH with SAA catalysts a promising technology for meeting the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术用于丙烯生产的主要优势包括：\n\n          1. 打破尺度关系：使用单原子合金（SAAs）的PDH可以同时提高丙烯选择性和丙烷转化率，克服了传统催化剂在活性和选择性之间的权衡。\n\n          2. 高选择性和转化率：SAA催化剂，特别是Pt/Cu SAA，可以在保持良好转化率的同时实现高丙烯选择性。\n\n          3. 高温下的优异稳定性：Pt/Cu SAA催化剂表现出卓越的稳定性，在大气压下高温（520°C）运行超过120小时。这比之前仅限于低温应用的SAA有了显著改进。\n\n          4. 提高效率：通过打破尺度关系，PDH技术解决了传统方法中通常会降低选择性的副反应问题。\n\n          5. 过程简化：与传统方法（如蒸汽裂解或流化催化裂解）相比，丙烷直接脱氢制丙烯是一个更简单的过程。\n\n          6. 成本效益：使用低铂载量（0.1wt%）的单原子合金在铜纳米粒子上，表明与传统的铂基催化剂相比，可能具有更高的成本效益。\n\n          这些优势直接解决了传统丙烯生产方法面临的原料利用效率、过程效率和产品选择性的挑战，使得采用SAA催化剂的PDH技术成为满足全球不断增长的丙烯需求的有前景的技术。", "Doi": "10.1038/s41467-018-06967-8"},

On-purpose production: PDH allows for targeted propylene manufacturing, addressing the strong demand for propylene specifically.\n\n2. Improved catalytic performance: The use of bimetallic catalysts, such as PtZn, leads to increased activity, improved product selectivity, and longer catalyst lifetime compared to conventional methods.\n\n3. Process simplification: Unlike some other processes, PDH does not require an additional hydrogen supply facility, which reduces costs and complexity.\n\n4. Feedstock flexibility: PDH directly uses propane as a feedstock, which is more readily available compared to the naphtha used in steam cracking.\n\n5. Higher selectivity: PDH can achieve very high propylene selectivity (>90% in some cases) compared to steam cracking, which produces a mixture of products.\n\n6. Stability and efficiency: PDH catalysts can show stable conversion close to thermodynamic equilibrium for extended periods (e.g., at least 63 hours) and very low deactivation rates (e.g., 0.4% conversion loss per day).\n\n7. Energy efficiency: The direct conversion of propane to propylene is potentially more energy-efficient than steam cracking, as it operates at lower temperatures.\n\n8. Potential for further improvement: Ongoing research on various catalyst supports and compositions suggests room for further optimization and performance enhancement in PDH technology.\n\nThese advantages collectively address the challenges of feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional production methods, making PDH a promising technology for meeting the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH允许针对性地生产丙烯，直接满足对丙烯的强劲需求。\n\n2. 改进的催化性能：使用双金属催化剂（如PtZn）可以提高活性，改善产品选择性，延长催化剂寿命，相比传统方法具有优势。\n\n3. 工艺简化：与其他一些工艺不同，PDH不需要额外的氢气供应设施，这降低了成本和复杂性。\n\n4. 原料灵活性：PDH直接使用丙烷作为原料，相比蒸汽裂解使用的石脑油更易获得。\n\n5. 更高的选择性：PDH可以实现非常高的丙烯选择性（在某些情况下>90%），而蒸汽裂解会生产混合产品。\n\n6. 稳定性和效率：PDH催化剂可以在较长时间内（例如至少63小时）保持接近热力学平衡的稳定转化，并且具有很低的失活率（例如每天0.4%的转化损失）。\n\n7. 能源效率：丙烷直接转化为丙烯的过程潜在地比蒸汽裂解更加节能，因为它在较低的温度下操作。\n\n8. 进一步改进的潜力：对各种催化剂载体和组成的持续研究表明，PDH技术在优化和性能提升方面还有进一步的空间。\n\n这些优势共同解决了传统生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战，使PDH成为满足不断增长的全球丙烯需求的一项有前景的技术。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.apcata.2006.03.028"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Propene is one of the most important base chemical intermediates mainly used in polymer and rubber industry. Process efficiency: PDH is a more targeted approach for propylene production compared to steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking, which produce a range of products.\n\n3. Product selectivity: While PDH faces challenges with selectivity due to high temperatures, it still offers better control over product composition compared to the broader product slate from conventional methods.\n\n4. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Non-oxidative PDH as an alternative route to propylene has received particular attention in recent years from industry and academia with the increasing exploration of cheap shale and natural gases\"\n\n[2] \"Till now, the productivity of propylene practiced by steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking processes derived from naphtha and crude oil can no longer meet the ever-growing demand\"\n\n[3] \"In addition, not only high energy-consuming is required, but also the emissions of CO2 and NOx contaminants are increased significantly during the foregoing two processes.\"\n\n[4] \"Currently, two representative of PtSn/Al2O3 (Oleflex) and CrOx/Al2O3 (Catofin) catalysts have been commercially applied in the PDH process\"\n\n[5] \"Such catalysts perform high activity and selectivity, but some corresponding drawbacks are accompanied, 1) the high-price of Pt and toxicity of Cr(VI); 2) the rapid deactivation caused by the sintering of metal particles and the coke deposition; 3) the successive regeneration resulting in activity attenuation and massive CO2 emissions.\"\n\n[6] \"To cater to the foregoing issues, numerous groups' efforts have been dedicated to design various catalysts, such as the supported catalysts with active metal oxides (e.g., CoOx, VOx, GaOx, and SnOx, etc.), which exhibit considerable activity and propylene selectivity in the PDH reaction. {"Quotes": "[1] \"The dehydrogenation of propane (DHP) to propylene represents an economical and environmentally friendly route compared to the traditional thermal or catalytic cracking of crude-oil-derived naphtha, which requires large amounts of energy and generates enormous CO2 emissions.\"\n\n          [2] \"An alumina-supported Pt catalyst is a vital component of the DHP process owing to its superior ability to activate paraffinic CH bonds and its low activity in CC bond cleavage.\"\n\n          [3] \"Nevertheless, the fast deactivation of the catalyst by coke deposition or Pt sintering is still a major problem.\"\n\n          [4] \"When used in the propane dehydrogenation reaction, this catalyst displayed an excellent specific activity for propylene formation with >99% selectivity, and superior anti-coking and anti-sintering properties.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n          1. Catalyst sintering: The high-temperature regeneration process can cause irreversible sintering of platinum catalysts.\n\n          Ongoing research aims to address these issues, particularly in developing catalysts that can improve selectivity while maintaining high conversion rates, making PDH a promising method for propylene production.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢(PDH)技术用于丙烯生产的主要优势包括：\n\n          1. 利用丰富的丙烷原料：PDH利用页岩气勘探带来的丙烷供应增加，解决了原料可用性的挑战。\n\n          2. 高转化效率：PDH在高温(>550°C)下运行，以实现高丙烷转化率，提高了工艺效率。\n\n          3. 直接生产路线：与传统方法相比，PDH提供了更直接的丙烯生产路线，可能提供更好的整体效率。\n\n          4. 催化剂创新：负载型铂催化剂对PDH具有高活性，尽管面临积碳和烧结的挑战。\n\n          然而，PDH技术也面临一些挑战：\n\n          1. 产品选择性：高温有利于不需要的副反应，如裂解和结焦，导致丙烯选择性低。\n\n          2. 催化剂失活：积碳导致催化剂失活，需要频繁再生。\n\n          3. 催化剂烧结：高温再生过程可能导致铂催化剂不可逆烧结。\n\n          正在进行的研究旨在解决这些问题，特别是开发能够在保持高转化率的同时提高选择性的催化剂，使PDH成为有前景的丙烯生产方法。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2018.08.001"},

It directly addresses the growing demand for propylene, providing a dedicated process for its production.\n\n2. PDH utilizes propane as feedstock, which is more readily available compared to traditional feedstocks used in other methods.\n\n3. The process offers higher selectivity towards propylene compared to conventional methods like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n4. PDH technology has already been commercialized, demonstrating its viability for industrial use.\n\n5. It provides better process efficiency as it's a single-step conversion from propane to propylene, unlike steam cracking which produces multiple products.\n\n6. Non-oxidative PDH avoids the thermodynamic equilibrium limitations present in oxidative dehydrogenation processes, potentially leading to higher yields.\n\n7. Current research focuses on developing novel catalysts (like V-, Ga-, and Sn-based) to overcome the limitations of traditional Pt- and Cr-based catalysts, potentially improving efficiency and reducing environmental impact.\n\n8. PDH offers more flexibility in production capacity, as plants can be scaled more easily than large steam crackers.\n\n9. It addresses the challenge of feedstock availability by utilizing propane, which is often a byproduct of other processes or available from shale gas processing.\n\nThese advantages collectively make PDH a versatile and potentially more sustainable option for meeting the growing propylene demand, especially in regions with abundant propane resources. It specifically addresses challenges in feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional propylene production methods.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为丙烯生产的一种有前景的方法：\n\n1. 它直接满足了丙烯不断增长的需求，提供了一种专门的生产过程。\n\n2. PDH使用丙烷作为原料，与其他方法使用的传统原料相比，丙烷更容易获得。\n\n3. 与传统方法（如蒸汽裂解或流化催化裂解）相比，该过程对丙烯的选择性更高。\n\n4. PDH技术已经在商业应用中实现，证明了其工业应用的可行性。\n\n5. 它提供了更好的工艺效率，因为它是从丙烷到丙烯的单步转化过程，不像蒸汽裂解那样产生多种产品。\n\n6. 非氧化PDH避免了氧化脱氢工艺中存在的热力学平衡限制，可能导致更高的产率。\n\n7. 目前的研究集中在开发新型催化剂（如基于V、Ga和Sn的催化剂）上，以克服传统Pt和Cr基催化剂的局限性，潜在地提高效率并减少环境影响。\n\n8. PDH在生产能力方面提供了更大的灵活性，因为工厂比大型蒸汽裂解装置更容易调整规模。\n\n9. 它通过利用丙烷（通常是其他过程的副产品或来自页岩气加工）解决了原料供应的挑战。\n\n这些优势共同使PDH成为一种versatile和潜在更可持续的选择，以满足不断增长的丙烯需求，特别是在丙烷资源丰富的地区。它具体解决了传统丙烯生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2017.12.004"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Light olefins are indispensable raw materials for numerous products. {"Quotes": "[1] \"A change of feedstock from naphtha to light alkanes, due to the emergence of shale gas and the increasing availability of natural gas, has led to an increasing development of on-purpose propane dehydrogenation (PDH) technologies.\"\n\n[2] \"PDH is an extremely energy-intensive process largely due to the high positive enthalpy of the reactions (ΔrH = 124 kJ mol1), necessitating high reaction temperatures,\"\n\n[3] \"which presents grand challenges for alkene selectivity and catalyst stability.\"\n\n[4] \"Especially, it has been shown that larger ensembles of active sites catalyze structure-sensitive side reactions, including cracking and deep dehydrogenation, leading to the production of C1 and C2 molecules and coke.\"\n\n[5] \"Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is a commercial propylene production technology, but high reaction temperatures result in cracking and coking.\"\n\n[6] \"Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is a commercial propylene production technology that has received much attention, but high reaction temperatures result in a decrease of propylene selectivity and catalyst stability.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology has emerged as the most promising method for propylene production due to several key advantages:\n\n1. Feedstock availability: PDH utilizes light alkanes, particularly propane, which are increasingly available due to the emergence of shale gas and natural gas resources. This addresses the challenge of feedstock availability faced by conventional naphtha-based production methods.\n\n2. On-purpose production: PDH is specifically designed for propylene production, allowing for more targeted and efficient production compared to traditional methods where propylene is often a byproduct.\n\n3. Process simplicity and flexibility: As a direct conversion process, PDH offers improved efficiency and greater flexibility in production capacity and location compared to more complex conventional routes.\n\n4. Independence from petroleum feedstocks: By using propane from natural gas sources, PDH reduces dependence on petroleum-based feedstocks, diversifying the propylene production supply chain.\n\n5. Potential for high selectivity: While PDH faces challenges in terms of alkene selectivity, advancements in catalyst design can potentially achieve high propylene selectivity.\n\nHowever, PDH technology also faces significant challenges:\n\n1. Energy intensity: The process is highly endothermic, requiring high reaction temperatures, which impacts energy efficiency.\n\n2. Selectivity issues: High temperatures can lead to unwanted side reactions like cracking and deep dehydrogenation, reducing propylene selectivity and producing unwanted byproducts and coke.\n\n3. Catalyst stability: The harsh reaction conditions can cause rapid catalyst deactivation, necessitating frequent regeneration or replacement.\n\nTo address these challenges, ongoing research focuses on developing more efficient catalysts that can operate at lower temperatures, improve propylene selectivity, and resist deactivation. The development of single-site catalysts is one approach to tackle these issues by inhibiting structure-sensitive side reactions and improving stability.\n\nOverall, while PDH technology offers significant advantages in terms of feedstock flexibility and on-purpose production, continuous research and development in catalyst design and process optimization are crucial to overcome its challenges and fully realize its potential as a leading method for propylene production.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术因其几个关键优势而成为丙烯生产的最有前景的方法：\n\n1. 原料可用性：PDH利用轻烷烃，特别是丙烷，这些原料由于页岩气和天然气资源的出现而日益丰富。这解决了传统基于石脑油生产方法面临的原料可用性挑战。\n\n2. 定向生产：PDH是专门为丙烯生产设计的技术，与传统方法相比（丙烯通常是副产品），允许更有针对性和高效的生产。\n\n3. 工艺简单和灵活性：作为直接转化过程，PDH提供了更高的效率，并在生产能力和位置方面提供了更大的灵活性，相比更复杂的传统路线。\n\n4. 独立于石油基原料：通过使用来自天然气源的丙烷，PDH减少了对石油基原料的依赖，使丙烯生产供应链多样化。\n\n5. 高选择性潜力：虽然PDH在烯烃选择性方面面临挑战，但催化剂设计的进步可能实现高丙烯选择性。\n\n然而，PDH技术也面临重大挑战：\n\n1. 能源密集：该过程高度吸热，需要高反应温度，影响能源效率。\n\n2. 选择性问题：高温可能导致不需要的副反应，如裂解和深度脱氢，降低丙烯选择性并产生不需要的副产品和焦炭。\n\n3. 催化剂稳定性：苛刻的反应条件可能导致催化剂快速失活，需要频繁再生或更换。\n\n为了解决这些挑战，正在进行的研究专注于开发更高效的催化剂，这些催化剂可以在较低温度下工作，提高丙烯选择性，并抵抗失活。单点催化剂的开发是解决这些问题的一种方法，通过抑制结构敏感的副反应和提高稳定性。\n\n总的来说，虽然PDH技术在原料灵活性和定向生产方面提供了显著的优势，但在催化剂设计和工艺优化方面的持续研究和开发对于克服其挑战并充分实现其作为丙烯生产主要方法的潜力至关重要。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.chempr.2020.10.008"},

Addresses supply shortfall: PDH directly targets the growing demand for propylene that outpaces ethylene demand and cannot be met by traditional steam cracking methods.\n\n          2. {"Quotes": "[1] \"In recent years, the ever-increasing demand for propylene has driven the rapid application and development of propane dehydrogenation technologies.\"\n\n[2] \"Theoretically, propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is an atom-economic reaction. That is, one mole of propane generates one mole propylene and one mole H2 through dehydrogenation, and both of the products are high value-added.\"\n\n[3] \"Obviously, increasing the conversion of propane for a single pass is an effective way to reduce the equipment investment and operation cost; however, it is not simple.\"\n\n[4] \"To increase the conversion of propane, from the view of thermodynamic equilibrium, there are three measures we can take: increasing the reaction temperature, reducing the partial pressure of hydrocarbons and lowering the partial pressure of H2.\"\n\n[5] \"There are two undesirable aspects of the dehydrogenation reaction: one is high energy consumption, i.e., the heat needed for the complete conversion of one mole of propane to propylene is approximately 120 kJ mol1; the other is that propane conversion for a single pass is not high due to the limitation of the thermodynamic equilibrium, and a large amount of unconverted propane must be recycled back to the reactor after separation, leading to large equipment investment and high energy consumption.\"\n\n[6] \"As for the development of the reactor, it should be noted that low operation pressure is beneficial for improving the single-pass conversion, decreasing the amount of unconverted alkane recycled back to the reactor, and reducing the energy consumption of the whole process.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology has emerged as the most promising method for propylene production due to several key advantages:\n\n1. This addresses the challenge of feedstock limitations faced by conventional methods.\n\n2. Atom economy and process efficiency: PDH is an atom-economic reaction, where one mole of propane generates one mole of propylene and one mole of hydrogen. Both products are high value-added, maximizing resource utilization and efficiency.\n\n3. Product selectivity: PDH offers high selectivity to propylene compared to other processes like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking, which produce a mix of olefins.\n\n4. {"Quotes": "[1] \"The catalytic dehydrogenation of propane to propylene could be carried out in the presence or absence of oxidants. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Light olefins are important building blocks in the chemical industry. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Because of their extensive use as chemical building blocks, light olefins, such as propylene (propene) and ethylene (ethene), are among the most important types of compounds in the chemical industry.\"\n\n[2] \"A number of factors including the high-energy demands of these processes, their low selectivity toward the production of particular olefins, dwindling petroleum reserves, and rising oil prices are driving the petrochemical industry to search for a more economical feedstock and more efficient conversion technologies.\"\n\n[3] \"Consequently, the recent boom in shale gas production has turned the United States into the lowest cost chemical producer outside the Middle East, as illustrated by the 126 investment projects totaling 84 billion dollars made up to September 2013 that have been tallied by the American Chemistry Council.\"\n\n[4] \"Indeed, the profitability of propane dehydrogenation is determined to a large extent by the price difference between propane and propylene, which makes the current market conditions very favorable. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Propylene serves as one of the most significant compounds in the chemical industry. Selectivity issues: Cracking reactions can still occur, affecting product selectivity.\n\nOngoing research aims to improve catalyst performance, process efficiency, and address these challenges to further enhance the advantages of PDH technology for meeting the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为一种有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH允许针对性地生产丙烯，以解决传统裂解方法（如流化催化裂化FCC）的供应短缺问题。\n\n2. 原料灵活性：它使用丙烷作为原料，相比蒸汽裂解中使用的石脑油或乙烷更容易获得。\n\n3. 工艺效率：作为直接转化工艺，PDH可能比生产多种产品的裂解方法提供更高的效率。\n\n4. 产品选择性：与裂解工艺相比，PDH对丙烯生产的选择性更高。\n\n5. 可扩展性：PDH装置可以按不同规模建造，以满足特定的市场需求。\n\n6. 独立于炼油厂操作：与FCC不同，PDH不依赖于炼油厂的操作，允许更灵活的生产。\n\n然而，PDH技术仍面临挑战，特别是在催化剂稳定性和结焦问题方面：\n\n1. 催化剂失活：结焦导致催化剂失活，需要频繁再生。\n\n2. 复杂性和成本：催化剂再生的需求增加了工艺的复杂性和成本。\n\n3. 选择性问题：裂解反应仍可能发生，影响产品选择性。\n\n持续的研究旨在改进催化剂性能、提高工艺效率，并解决这些挑战，以进一步增强PDH技术在满足全球不断增长的丙烯需求方面的优势。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2008.11.014"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Among the emerging methods, the PDH process has garnered interest as the most efficient process that can meet the large demand for propylene\"\n\n[2] \"A major problem of the PDH process, however, is that the reaction requires high-temperature operations, at 773 K or higher, to increase the thermodynamic equilibrium limit\"\n\n[3] \"Until recent years, the industrial demand for ethylene and propylene was satisfied with a balance by large-scale production from naphtha crackers\"\n\n[4] \"However, a new and less expensive source of ethylene recently became available in increasing amounts from ethane cracking in natural gas and shale gas\"\n\n[5] \"This broke the previous ethylene-propylene production balance, causing a need to find proper on-purpose methods for propylene production, such as catalytic propane dehydrogenation (PDH), olefin metathesis, and methanol-to-olefin processes\"\n\n[6] \"Typically, the PDH process employs a Pt-Sn bimetallic catalyst supported on porous alumina (PtSn/Al2O3) or chromium oxide-supported alumina (CrOx/Al2O3), but both suffer from rapid deactivation due to coke deposition\"\n\n[7] \"Of the two typical catalysts, CrOx/Al2O3 has disadvantages of chromium toxicity and rapid deactivation (approximately in 15 min), which can be overcome by catalyst regeneration by a simple air-burning process\"\n\n[8] \"On the other hand, the employed PtSn/Al2O3 catalyst requires frequent regeneration (typically, every 5 d), but the regeneration involves a high-temperature treatment with a toxic and corrosive gas mixture containing O2 and HCl\"", "English": "The key advantages of propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology that make it the most promising method for propylene production are:\n\n1. {"Quotes": "\"Direct dehydrogenation can be performed either with or without an oxidant present, and O2, CO2 and N2O can all participate as oxidants to form propene from propane. The discovery of active and selective catalysts is central to the development of these on-purpose technologies and is the focus of the current review.\"\n\n\"Annual propene production was around 130 megatonnes in 2019 and is predicted to increase to 191 megatonnes by 2030. Significantly, the expected growth in propane demand cannot be met by existing processes, which are based on steam-cracking (SC) and fluid catalytic cracking (FCC). Instead, direct or on-purpose processes are being developed to fill the so-called propene gap.\"\n\n\"The direct formation of propene from propane is a well-established commercial process, which on the basis of energy consumption, is environmentally preferred to the current large-scale sources of propene from steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking.\"\n\n\"At present, sources of propane are mostly non-renewable, but the development of technologies to produce renewable green propane are gaining traction, which coupled with new catalytic processes will provide the platform to produce green propene.\"\n\n\"Direct propane dehydrogenation satisfies many principles of green chemistry in comparison to SC and MTO benchmarks: it is highly atom-economic, does not use toxic reactants (or generate toxic by-products) and can in principle, utilise renewable feedstocks.\"\n\n\"DDH is to date the only reaction that has been operated commercially. The most active catalysts reported in the literature are based on chromium oxide or platinum promoted with tin oxide, but even these require frequent regeneration due to coking.\"\n\n\"In the case of dehydrogenation only H2 is generated as a by-product, meaning an atom economy of 95% is possible.\"\n\n\"From an environmental perspective, ODH-CO2 has the greatest potential in the context of a circular economy. Although the formation of water is less desirable than hydrogen, ODH-CO2 has the benefit of consuming CO2 in the process, and this is often cited as the motivation for investigating this route.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n1. On-purpose production: PDH is specifically designed to produce propylene, addressing the growing demand that cannot be met by existing processes like steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n2. Energy efficiency: PDH is more environmentally friendly in terms of energy consumption compared to traditional methods.\n\n3. Feedstock flexibility: PDH can utilize propane from various sources, including potential renewable sources in the future.\n\n4. High atom economy: PDH has a very high atom economy of up to 95%, making it highly efficient in terms of raw material utilization.\n\n5. Environmental benefits: PDH does not use toxic reactants or generate toxic by-products, and it can potentially use renewable feedstocks.\n\n6. Process flexibility: PDH can be performed with or without oxidants, allowing for process optimization based on specific requirements.\n\n7. Commercial viability: PDH is the only direct dehydrogenation process that has been successfully commercialized.\n\n8. Catalyst innovation: Ongoing research into active and selective catalysts is improving the efficiency and selectivity of PDH processes.\n\n9. Potential for sustainability: PDH technology can be coupled with emerging green propane production methods to create a more sustainable propylene production process.\n\nThese advantages address the challenges faced by conventional production methods in terms of feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity. PDH offers a more targeted, efficient, and potentially sustainable approach to propylene production, with the flexibility to adapt to changing feedstock availability and environmental concerns.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH专门设计用于生产丙烯，解决了现有工艺如蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解无法满足的不断增长的需求。\n\n2. 能源效率：与传统方法相比，PDH在能源消耗方面更加环保。\n\n3. 原料灵活性：PDH可以利用来自各种来源的丙烷，包括未来潜在的可再生来源。\n\n4. 高原子经济性：PDH具有高达95%的原子经济性，使其在原材料利用方面非常高效。\n\n5. 环境效益：PDH不使用有毒反应物或产生有毒副产品，并且可以潜在地使用可再生原料。\n\n6. 工艺灵活性：PDH可以在有或没有氧化剂的情况下进行，允许根据具体要求进行工艺优化。\n\n7. 商业可行性：PDH是唯一成功商业化的直接脱氢工艺。\n\n8. 催化剂创新：对活性和选择性催化剂的持续研究正在提高PDH工艺的效率和选择性。\n\n9. 可持续性潜力：PDH技术可以与新兴的绿色丙烷生产方法相结合，创造更可持续的丙烯生产工艺。\n\n这些优势解决了传统生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战。PDH提供了一种更有针对性、更高效和潜在更可持续的丙烯生产方法，具有适应不断变化的原料供应和环境问题的灵活性。", "Doi": "10.1039/D1GC03700E"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Noble-metal alloys are widely used as heterogeneous catalysts. However, due to the existence of scaling properties of adsorption energies on transition metal surfaces, the enhancement of catalytic activity is frequently accompanied by side reactions leading to a reduction in selectivity for the target product.\"\n\n          [2] \"Herein, we describe an approach to breaking the scaling relationship for propane dehydrogenation, an industrially important reaction, by assembling single atom alloys (SAAs), to achieve simultaneous enhancement of propylene selectivity and propane conversion.\"\n\n          [3] \"Unlike previous reported SAA applications at low temperatures (<400C), Pt/Cu SAA shows excellent stability of more than 120h of operation under atmospheric pressure at 520C.\"", "English": "The key advantages of propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology for propylene production include:\n\n          1. Breaking the scaling relationship: PDH using single atom alloys (SAAs) can simultaneously enhance propylene selectivity and propane conversion, overcoming the trade-off between activity and selectivity faced by conventional catalysts.\n\n          2. High selectivity and conversion: SAA catalysts, particularly Pt/Cu SAA, can achieve high propylene selectivity while maintaining good conversion rates.\n\n          3. Excellent stability at high temperatures: Pt/Cu SAA catalysts demonstrate exceptional stability, operating for over 120 hours at high temperatures (520°C) under atmospheric pressure. This is a significant improvement over previous SAA applications that were limited to lower temperatures.\n\n          4. Improved efficiency: By breaking the scaling relationship, PDH technology addresses the challenge of side reactions that typically reduce selectivity in conventional methods.\n\n          5. Process simplification: Direct dehydrogenation of propane to propylene is a simpler process compared to conventional methods like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n          6. Cost-effectiveness: The use of single atom alloys with a low platinum loading (0.1wt%) on copper nanoparticles suggests a potentially more cost-effective catalyst compared to traditional platinum-based catalysts.\n\n          These advantages directly address the challenges of feedstock utilization efficiency, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional propylene production methods, making PDH with SAA catalysts a promising technology for meeting the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术用于丙烯生产的主要优势包括：\n\n          1. 打破尺度关系：使用单原子合金（SAAs）的PDH可以同时提高丙烯选择性和丙烷转化率，克服了传统催化剂在活性和选择性之间的权衡。\n\n          2. 高选择性和转化率：SAA催化剂，特别是Pt/Cu SAA，可以在保持良好转化率的同时实现高丙烯选择性。\n\n          3. 高温下的优异稳定性：Pt/Cu SAA催化剂表现出卓越的稳定性，在大气压下高温（520°C）运行超过120小时。这比之前仅限于低温应用的SAA有了显著改进。\n\n          4. 提高效率：通过打破尺度关系，PDH技术解决了传统方法中通常会降低选择性的副反应问题。\n\n          5. 过程简化：与传统方法（如蒸汽裂解或流化催化裂解）相比，丙烷直接脱氢制丙烯是一个更简单的过程。\n\n          6. 成本效益：使用低铂载量（0.1wt%）的单原子合金在铜纳米粒子上，表明与传统的铂基催化剂相比，可能具有更高的成本效益。\n\n          这些优势直接解决了传统丙烯生产方法面临的原料利用效率、过程效率和产品选择性的挑战，使得采用SAA催化剂的PDH技术成为满足全球不断增长的丙烯需求的有前景的技术。", "Doi": "10.1038/s41467-018-06967-8"},

On-purpose production: PDH allows for targeted propylene manufacturing, addressing the strong demand for propylene specifically.\n\n2. Improved catalytic performance: The use of bimetallic catalysts, such as PtZn, leads to increased activity, improved product selectivity, and longer catalyst lifetime compared to conventional methods.\n\n3. Process simplification: Unlike some other processes, PDH does not require an additional hydrogen supply facility, which reduces costs and complexity.\n\n4. Feedstock flexibility: PDH directly uses propane as a feedstock, which is more readily available compared to the naphtha used in steam cracking.\n\n5. Higher selectivity: PDH can achieve very high propylene selectivity (>90% in some cases) compared to steam cracking, which produces a mixture of products.\n\n6. Stability and efficiency: PDH catalysts can show stable conversion close to thermodynamic equilibrium for extended periods (e.g., at least 63 hours) and very low deactivation rates (e.g., 0.4% conversion loss per day).\n\n7. Energy efficiency: The direct conversion of propane to propylene is potentially more energy-efficient than steam cracking, as it operates at lower temperatures.\n\n8. Potential for further improvement: Ongoing research on various catalyst supports and compositions suggests room for further optimization and performance enhancement in PDH technology.\n\nThese advantages collectively address the challenges of feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional production methods, making PDH a promising technology for meeting the growing global demand for propylene.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 定向生产：PDH允许针对性地生产丙烯，直接满足对丙烯的强劲需求。\n\n2. 改进的催化性能：使用双金属催化剂（如PtZn）可以提高活性，改善产品选择性，延长催化剂寿命，相比传统方法具有优势。\n\n3. 工艺简化：与其他一些工艺不同，PDH不需要额外的氢气供应设施，这降低了成本和复杂性。\n\n4. 原料灵活性：PDH直接使用丙烷作为原料，相比蒸汽裂解使用的石脑油更易获得。\n\n5. 更高的选择性：PDH可以实现非常高的丙烯选择性（在某些情况下>90%），而蒸汽裂解会生产混合产品。\n\n6. 稳定性和效率：PDH催化剂可以在较长时间内（例如至少63小时）保持接近热力学平衡的稳定转化，并且具有很低的失活率（例如每天0.4%的转化损失）。\n\n7. 能源效率：丙烷直接转化为丙烯的过程潜在地比蒸汽裂解更加节能，因为它在较低的温度下操作。\n\n8. 进一步改进的潜力：对各种催化剂载体和组成的持续研究表明，PDH技术在优化和性能提升方面还有进一步的空间。\n\n这些优势共同解决了传统生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战，使PDH成为满足不断增长的全球丙烯需求的一项有前景的技术。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.apcata.2006.03.028"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Propene is one of the most important base chemical intermediates mainly used in polymer and rubber industry. Process efficiency: PDH is a more targeted approach for propylene production compared to steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking, which produce a range of products.\n\n3. Product selectivity: While PDH faces challenges with selectivity due to high temperatures, it still offers better control over product composition compared to the broader product slate from conventional methods.\n\n4. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Non-oxidative PDH as an alternative route to propylene has received particular attention in recent years from industry and academia with the increasing exploration of cheap shale and natural gases\"\n\n[2] \"Till now, the productivity of propylene practiced by steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking processes derived from naphtha and crude oil can no longer meet the ever-growing demand\"\n\n[3] \"In addition, not only high energy-consuming is required, but also the emissions of CO2 and NOx contaminants are increased significantly during the foregoing two processes.\"\n\n[4] \"Currently, two representative of PtSn/Al2O3 (Oleflex) and CrOx/Al2O3 (Catofin) catalysts have been commercially applied in the PDH process\"\n\n[5] \"Such catalysts perform high activity and selectivity, but some corresponding drawbacks are accompanied, 1) the high-price of Pt and toxicity of Cr(VI); 2) the rapid deactivation caused by the sintering of metal particles and the coke deposition; 3) the successive regeneration resulting in activity attenuation and massive CO2 emissions.\"\n\n[6] \"To cater to the foregoing issues, numerous groups' efforts have been dedicated to design various catalysts, such as the supported catalysts with active metal oxides (e.g., CoOx, VOx, GaOx, and SnOx, etc.), which exhibit considerable activity and propylene selectivity in the PDH reaction. {"Quotes": "[1] \"The dehydrogenation of propane (DHP) to propylene represents an economical and environmentally friendly route compared to the traditional thermal or catalytic cracking of crude-oil-derived naphtha, which requires large amounts of energy and generates enormous CO2 emissions.\"\n\n          [2] \"An alumina-supported Pt catalyst is a vital component of the DHP process owing to its superior ability to activate paraffinic CH bonds and its low activity in CC bond cleavage.\"\n\n          [3] \"Nevertheless, the fast deactivation of the catalyst by coke deposition or Pt sintering is still a major problem.\"\n\n          [4] \"When used in the propane dehydrogenation reaction, this catalyst displayed an excellent specific activity for propylene formation with >99% selectivity, and superior anti-coking and anti-sintering properties.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology offers several key advantages that make it the most promising method for propylene production:\n\n          1. Catalyst sintering: The high-temperature regeneration process can cause irreversible sintering of platinum catalysts.\n\n          Ongoing research aims to address these issues, particularly in developing catalysts that can improve selectivity while maintaining high conversion rates, making PDH a promising method for propylene production.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢(PDH)技术用于丙烯生产的主要优势包括：\n\n          1. 利用丰富的丙烷原料：PDH利用页岩气勘探带来的丙烷供应增加，解决了原料可用性的挑战。\n\n          2. 高转化效率：PDH在高温(>550°C)下运行，以实现高丙烷转化率，提高了工艺效率。\n\n          3. 直接生产路线：与传统方法相比，PDH提供了更直接的丙烯生产路线，可能提供更好的整体效率。\n\n          4. 催化剂创新：负载型铂催化剂对PDH具有高活性，尽管面临积碳和烧结的挑战。\n\n          然而，PDH技术也面临一些挑战：\n\n          1. 产品选择性：高温有利于不需要的副反应，如裂解和结焦，导致丙烯选择性低。\n\n          2. 催化剂失活：积碳导致催化剂失活，需要频繁再生。\n\n          3. 催化剂烧结：高温再生过程可能导致铂催化剂不可逆烧结。\n\n          正在进行的研究旨在解决这些问题，特别是开发能够在保持高转化率的同时提高选择性的催化剂，使PDH成为有前景的丙烯生产方法。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2018.08.001"},

It directly addresses the growing demand for propylene, providing a dedicated process for its production.\n\n2. PDH utilizes propane as feedstock, which is more readily available compared to traditional feedstocks used in other methods.\n\n3. The process offers higher selectivity towards propylene compared to conventional methods like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking.\n\n4. PDH technology has already been commercialized, demonstrating its viability for industrial use.\n\n5. It provides better process efficiency as it's a single-step conversion from propane to propylene, unlike steam cracking which produces multiple products.\n\n6. Non-oxidative PDH avoids the thermodynamic equilibrium limitations present in oxidative dehydrogenation processes, potentially leading to higher yields.\n\n7. Current research focuses on developing novel catalysts (like V-, Ga-, and Sn-based) to overcome the limitations of traditional Pt- and Cr-based catalysts, potentially improving efficiency and reducing environmental impact.\n\n8. PDH offers more flexibility in production capacity, as plants can be scaled more easily than large steam crackers.\n\n9. It addresses the challenge of feedstock availability by utilizing propane, which is often a byproduct of other processes or available from shale gas processing.\n\nThese advantages collectively make PDH a versatile and potentially more sustainable option for meeting the growing propylene demand, especially in regions with abundant propane resources. It specifically addresses challenges in feedstock availability, process efficiency, and product selectivity faced by conventional propylene production methods.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为丙烯生产的一种有前景的方法：\n\n1. 它直接满足了丙烯不断增长的需求，提供了一种专门的生产过程。\n\n2. PDH使用丙烷作为原料，与其他方法使用的传统原料相比，丙烷更容易获得。\n\n3. 与传统方法（如蒸汽裂解或流化催化裂解）相比，该过程对丙烯的选择性更高。\n\n4. PDH技术已经在商业应用中实现，证明了其工业应用的可行性。\n\n5. 它提供了更好的工艺效率，因为它是从丙烷到丙烯的单步转化过程，不像蒸汽裂解那样产生多种产品。\n\n6. 非氧化PDH避免了氧化脱氢工艺中存在的热力学平衡限制，可能导致更高的产率。\n\n7. 目前的研究集中在开发新型催化剂（如基于V、Ga和Sn的催化剂）上，以克服传统Pt和Cr基催化剂的局限性，潜在地提高效率并减少环境影响。\n\n8. PDH在生产能力方面提供了更大的灵活性，因为工厂比大型蒸汽裂解装置更容易调整规模。\n\n9. 它通过利用丙烷（通常是其他过程的副产品或来自页岩气加工）解决了原料供应的挑战。\n\n这些优势共同使PDH成为一种versatile和潜在更可持续的选择，以满足不断增长的丙烯需求，特别是在丙烷资源丰富的地区。它具体解决了传统丙烯生产方法在原料可用性、工艺效率和产品选择性方面面临的挑战。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2017.12.004"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Light olefins are indispensable raw materials for numerous products. {"Quotes": "[1] \"A change of feedstock from naphtha to light alkanes, due to the emergence of shale gas and the increasing availability of natural gas, has led to an increasing development of on-purpose propane dehydrogenation (PDH) technologies.\"\n\n[2] \"PDH is an extremely energy-intensive process largely due to the high positive enthalpy of the reactions (ΔrH = 124 kJ mol1), necessitating high reaction temperatures,\"\n\n[3] \"which presents grand challenges for alkene selectivity and catalyst stability.\"\n\n[4] \"Especially, it has been shown that larger ensembles of active sites catalyze structure-sensitive side reactions, including cracking and deep dehydrogenation, leading to the production of C1 and C2 molecules and coke.\"\n\n[5] \"Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is a commercial propylene production technology, but high reaction temperatures result in cracking and coking.\"\n\n[6] \"Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is a commercial propylene production technology that has received much attention, but high reaction temperatures result in a decrease of propylene selectivity and catalyst stability.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology has emerged as the most promising method for propylene production due to several key advantages:\n\n1. Feedstock availability: PDH utilizes light alkanes, particularly propane, which are increasingly available due to the emergence of shale gas and natural gas resources. This addresses the challenge of feedstock availability faced by conventional naphtha-based production methods.\n\n2. On-purpose production: PDH is specifically designed for propylene production, allowing for more targeted and efficient production compared to traditional methods where propylene is often a byproduct.\n\n3. Process simplicity and flexibility: As a direct conversion process, PDH offers improved efficiency and greater flexibility in production capacity and location compared to more complex conventional routes.\n\n4. Independence from petroleum feedstocks: By using propane from natural gas sources, PDH reduces dependence on petroleum-based feedstocks, diversifying the propylene production supply chain.\n\n5. Potential for high selectivity: While PDH faces challenges in terms of alkene selectivity, advancements in catalyst design can potentially achieve high propylene selectivity.\n\nHowever, PDH technology also faces significant challenges:\n\n1. Energy intensity: The process is highly endothermic, requiring high reaction temperatures, which impacts energy efficiency.\n\n2. Selectivity issues: High temperatures can lead to unwanted side reactions like cracking and deep dehydrogenation, reducing propylene selectivity and producing unwanted byproducts and coke.\n\n3. Catalyst stability: The harsh reaction conditions can cause rapid catalyst deactivation, necessitating frequent regeneration or replacement.\n\nTo address these challenges, ongoing research focuses on developing more efficient catalysts that can operate at lower temperatures, improve propylene selectivity, and resist deactivation. The development of single-site catalysts is one approach to tackle these issues by inhibiting structure-sensitive side reactions and improving stability.\n\nOverall, while PDH technology offers significant advantages in terms of feedstock flexibility and on-purpose production, continuous research and development in catalyst design and process optimization are crucial to overcome its challenges and fully realize its potential as a leading method for propylene production.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术因其几个关键优势而成为丙烯生产的最有前景的方法：\n\n1. 原料可用性：PDH利用轻烷烃，特别是丙烷，这些原料由于页岩气和天然气资源的出现而日益丰富。这解决了传统基于石脑油生产方法面临的原料可用性挑战。\n\n2. 定向生产：PDH是专门为丙烯生产设计的技术，与传统方法相比（丙烯通常是副产品），允许更有针对性和高效的生产。\n\n3. 工艺简单和灵活性：作为直接转化过程，PDH提供了更高的效率，并在生产能力和位置方面提供了更大的灵活性，相比更复杂的传统路线。\n\n4. 独立于石油基原料：通过使用来自天然气源的丙烷，PDH减少了对石油基原料的依赖，使丙烯生产供应链多样化。\n\n5. 高选择性潜力：虽然PDH在烯烃选择性方面面临挑战，但催化剂设计的进步可能实现高丙烯选择性。\n\n然而，PDH技术也面临重大挑战：\n\n1. 能源密集：该过程高度吸热，需要高反应温度，影响能源效率。\n\n2. 选择性问题：高温可能导致不需要的副反应，如裂解和深度脱氢，降低丙烯选择性并产生不需要的副产品和焦炭。\n\n3. 催化剂稳定性：苛刻的反应条件可能导致催化剂快速失活，需要频繁再生或更换。\n\n为了解决这些挑战，正在进行的研究专注于开发更高效的催化剂，这些催化剂可以在较低温度下工作，提高丙烯选择性，并抵抗失活。单点催化剂的开发是解决这些问题的一种方法，通过抑制结构敏感的副反应和提高稳定性。\n\n总的来说，虽然PDH技术在原料灵活性和定向生产方面提供了显著的优势，但在催化剂设计和工艺优化方面的持续研究和开发对于克服其挑战并充分实现其作为丙烯生产主要方法的潜力至关重要。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.chempr.2020.10.008"},

Addresses supply shortfall: PDH directly targets the growing demand for propylene that outpaces ethylene demand and cannot be met by traditional steam cracking methods.\n\n          2. {"Quotes": "[1] \"In recent years, the ever-increasing demand for propylene has driven the rapid application and development of propane dehydrogenation technologies.\"\n\n[2] \"Theoretically, propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is an atom-economic reaction. That is, one mole of propane generates one mole propylene and one mole H2 through dehydrogenation, and both of the products are high value-added.\"\n\n[3] \"Obviously, increasing the conversion of propane for a single pass is an effective way to reduce the equipment investment and operation cost; however, it is not simple.\"\n\n[4] \"To increase the conversion of propane, from the view of thermodynamic equilibrium, there are three measures we can take: increasing the reaction temperature, reducing the partial pressure of hydrocarbons and lowering the partial pressure of H2.\"\n\n[5] \"There are two undesirable aspects of the dehydrogenation reaction: one is high energy consumption, i.e., the heat needed for the complete conversion of one mole of propane to propylene is approximately 120 kJ mol1; the other is that propane conversion for a single pass is not high due to the limitation of the thermodynamic equilibrium, and a large amount of unconverted propane must be recycled back to the reactor after separation, leading to large equipment investment and high energy consumption.\"\n\n[6] \"As for the development of the reactor, it should be noted that low operation pressure is beneficial for improving the single-pass conversion, decreasing the amount of unconverted alkane recycled back to the reactor, and reducing the energy consumption of the whole process.\"", "English": "Propane direct dehydrogenation (PDH) technology has emerged as the most promising method for propylene production due to several key advantages:\n\n1. This addresses the challenge of feedstock limitations faced by conventional methods.\n\n2. Atom economy and process efficiency: PDH is an atom-economic reaction, where one mole of propane generates one mole of propylene and one mole of hydrogen. Both products are high value-added, maximizing resource utilization and efficiency.\n\n3. Product selectivity: PDH offers high selectivity to propylene compared to other processes like steam cracking or fluid catalytic cracking, which produce a mix of olefins.\n\n4. {"Quotes": "[1] \"The catalytic dehydrogenation of propane to propylene could be carried out in the presence or absence of oxidants. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Light olefins are important building blocks in the chemical industry. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Because of their extensive use as chemical building blocks, light olefins, such as propylene (propene) and ethylene (ethene), are among the most important types of compounds in the chemical industry.\"\n\n[2] \"A number of factors including the high-energy demands of these processes, their low selectivity toward the production of particular olefins, dwindling petroleum reserves, and rising oil prices are driving the petrochemical industry to search for a more economical feedstock and more efficient conversion technologies.\"\n\n[3] \"Consequently, the recent boom in shale gas production has turned the United States into the lowest cost chemical producer outside the Middle East, as illustrated by the 126 investment projects totaling 84 billion dollars made up to September 2013 that have been tallied by the American Chemistry Council.\"\n\n[4] \"Indeed, the profitability of propane dehydrogenation is determined to a large extent by the price difference between propane and propylene, which makes the current market conditions very favorable. Process efficiency: PDH offers a more direct and efficient route to produce propylene from propane, compared to the multi-step processes involved in conventional methods.\n\n6. Versatility: Propylene produced through PDH can be used in the synthesis of various valuable chemicals, including polypropylene, acrylic acid, and acrylonitrile.\n\nThese advantages allow PDH to address the challenges faced by conventional production methods in terms of feedstock availability (by utilizing abundant propane), process efficiency (through a more direct conversion process), and product selectivity (by offering higher propylene selectivity). PDH technology provides a more efficient, selective, and economically viable solution for propylene production compared to conventional methods, while also meeting the increasing global demand for this vital petrochemical building block.", "Chinese": "丙烷直接脱氢（PDH）技术提供了几个关键优势，使其成为最有前景的丙烯生产方法：\n\n1. 高丙烯选择性：与流化催化裂化（FCC）和石脑油蒸汽裂解等传统方法相比，PDH提供了显著更高的丙烯选择性。\n\n2. 原料可用性：随着页岩气和天然气水合物开采技术的发展，丙烷变得更加丰富和便宜，使PDH在经济上更加可行。\n\n3. 较低的能源消耗：与能耗高的FCC和蒸汽裂解不同，PDH通常更加节能。\n\n4. 满足不断增长的需求：传统方法难以满足不断增长的丙烯需求，而PDH有潜力弥补这一差距。\n\n5. 工艺效率：与传统方法涉及的多步骤过程相比，PDH提供了一种更直接、更高效的从丙烷生产丙烯的路径。\n\n6. 多用途性：通过PDH生产的丙烯可用于合成各种有价值的化学品，包括聚丙烯、丙烯酸和丙烯腈。\n\n这些优势使PDH能够解决传统生产方法在原料可用性（通过利用丰富的丙烷）、工艺效率（通过更直接的转化过程）和产品选择性（通过提供更高的丙烯选择性）方面面临的挑战。PDH技术为丙烯生产提供了更高效、更具选择性和更具经济可行性的解决方案，同时还能满足这种重要石化基础原料日益增长的全球需求。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.mcat.2022.112580"},
